  match access-group name AUTOQOS-ACL-DEFAULT
class-map match-all AUTOQOS_VOIP_SIGNAL_CLASS
  match ip dscp cs3
!
policy-map AUTOQOS-SRND4-CISCOPHONE-POLICY
 class AUTOQOS_VOIP_DATA_CLASS
   set dscp ef
  police 128000 8000 exceed-action policed-dscp-transmit
 class AUTOQOS_VOIP_SIGNAL_CLASS
   set dscp cs3
  police 32000 8000 exceed-action policed-dscp-transmit
 class AUTOQOS_DEFAULT_CLASS
   set dscp default
  police 10000000 8000 exceed-action policed-dscp-transmit
!
!

!
!

macro name NO-DOT1X
#802.1X Wired Macro-apply configuration on protected  switch ports
 no switchport mode access
 no authentication event server dead action authorize vlan 555
 no authentication event fail action authorize vlan 555
 no authentication event no-response action authorize vlan 555
 no authentication port-control auto
 no authentication order dot1x mab
 no authentication priority dot1x mab
 no authentication timer reauthenticate server
 no dot1x pae authenticator
 no dot1x timeout server-timeout 60
 no dot1x timeout tx-period 5
 no dot1x max-req 1
 no mab
@
macro name DOT1X
#802.1X Wired Macro-apply configuration on protected  switch ports
switchport access vlan 401
switchport mode access
switchport voice vlan 501
authentication event server dead action authorize vlan 555
authentication event fail action authorize vlan 555
authentication event no-response action authorize vlan 555

authentication host-mode multi-host

authentication timer reauthenticate server
dot1x pae authenticator
dot1x timeout server-timeout 60
dot1x timeout tx-period 5
dot1x max-req 1
mab
spanning-tree portfast
auto qos voip cisco-phone
@
